## Idea

Consider a span `ùíÆ` of types

```text
      f     g
  A <--- S ---> B.
```

and a type `X` equipped with a
[cocone structure](synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.md) of `S` into
`X`. The **universal property of the pushout** of `ùíÆ` asserts that `X` is the
_initial_ type equipped with such cocone structure. In other words, the
universal property of the pushout of `ùíÆ` asserts that the following evaluation
map is an equivalence:

```text
  (X ‚Üí Y) ‚Üí cocone ùíÆ Y.
```

There are several ways of asserting a condition equivalent to the universal
property of pushouts:

1. The universal property of pushouts
2. The
   [pullback property of pushouts](synthetic-homotopy-theory.pullback-property-pushouts.md).
   This is a restatement of the universal property of pushouts in terms of
   pullbacks.
3. The
   [dependent universal property of pushouts](synthetic-homotopy-theory.dependent-universal-property-pushouts.md).
   This property characterizes _dependent_ functions out of a pushout
4. The
   [dependent pullback property of pushouts](synthetic-homotopy-theory.dependent-pullback-property-pushouts.md).
   This is a restatement of the dependent universal property of pushouts in
   terms of pullbacks
5. The
   [induction principle of pushouts](synthetic-homotopy-theory.induction-principle-pushouts.md).
   This weaker form of the dependent universal property of pushouts expresses
   the induction principle of pushouts seen as higher inductive types.

## Properties

### The 3-for-2 property of pushouts

    <a id="8171" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8173" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#6134" class="Function">is-equiv-up-pushout-up-pushout</a> <a id="8204" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7917" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8206" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7919" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="8208" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7921" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8210" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7923" class="Bound">d</a>
      <a id="8218" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8220" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#3387" class="Function">map-universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="8251" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7917" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8253" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7919" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="8255" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7921" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8257" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7925" class="Bound">up-c</a> <a id="8262" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7923" class="Bound">d</a><a id="8263" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="8271" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8273" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#3492" class="Function">htpy-cocone-map-universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="8316" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7917" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8318" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7919" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="8320" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7921" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8322" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7925" class="Bound">up-c</a> <a id="8327" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7923" class="Bound">d</a><a id="8328" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="8336" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8338" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7925" class="Bound">up-c</a><a id="8342" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="8350" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8352" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#7930" class="Bound">up-d</a><a id="8356" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### The universal property of pushouts is equivalent to the pullback property of pushouts

In order to show that the universal property of pushouts is equivalent to the
pullback property, we show that the maps `cocone-map` and the gap map fit in a
commuting triangle, where the third map is an equivalence. The claim then
follows from the 3-for-2 property of equivalences.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="triangle-pullback-property-pushout-universal-property-pushout"></a><a id="8746" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#8746" class="Function">triangle-pullback-property-pushout-universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="8808" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="10309" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#9806" class="Function">is-equiv-left-map-triangle</a>

        <a id="10619" href="foundation-core.functoriality-dependent-pair-types.html#6043" class="Function">is-equiv-tot-is-fiberwise-equiv</a> <a id="10651" class="Symbol">(Œª</a> <a id="10654" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10654" class="Bound">j&#39;</a> <a id="10657" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10659" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#2791" class="Postulate">funext</a> <a id="10666" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10667" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10606" class="Bound">i&#39;</a> <a id="10670" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="10672" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10292" class="Bound">f</a><a id="10673" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10675" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10676" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10654" class="Bound">j&#39;</a> <a id="10679" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="10681" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10294" class="Bound">g</a><a id="10682" class="Symbol">))))</a>
</pre>
### If the vertical map of a span is an equivalence, then the vertical map of a cocone on it is an equivalence if and only if the cocone is a pushout

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-equiv-universal-property-pushout"></a><a id="10851" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10851" class="Function">is-equiv-universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="10887" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="10891" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10892" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10892" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="10895" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="10911" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10913" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10914" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10914" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10892" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="10923" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10925" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10926" id="10933" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10895" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="10935" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10937" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10938" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#10938" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="10940" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10942" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a   <a id="12201" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1647" class="Function">is-equiv</a> <a id="12210" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12155" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12212" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="12214" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1647" class="Function">is-equiv</a> <a id="12223" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12224" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#1873" class="Function">vertical-map-cocone</a> <a id="12244" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12155" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12246" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12167" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="12248" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12179" class="Bound">c</a><a id="12249" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12251" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a>
  <a id="12255" class="Symbol">({</a><a id="12257" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12257" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="12259" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12261" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="12266" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12268" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="12270" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#2873" class="Function">universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="12297" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12257" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="12299" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12155" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12301" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12167" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="12303" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12179" class="Bound">c</a><a id="12304" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="12344" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12344" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12346" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12346" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="12348" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12349" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12349" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12351" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#689" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12353" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12353" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="12355" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#689" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12357" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12357" class="Bound">H</a><a id="12358" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12360" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12360" class="Bound">is-equiv-f</a> <a id="12371" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12371" class="Bound">is-equiv-j</a> <a id="12382" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12383" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12383" class="Bound">l</a><a id="12384" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12386" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="12390" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="12394" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12394" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="12396" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12398" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12399" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12349" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12401" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#689" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12403" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12353" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="12405" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#689" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12407" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12357" class="Bound">H</a><a id="12408" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12410" class="Keyword">in</a>
  <a id="12415" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#9978" class="Function">universal-property-pushout-pullback-property-pushout</a> <a id="12468" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12383" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="12470" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12344" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12472" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12346" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="12474" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12394" class="Bound">c</a>
    <a id="12480" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12482" class="Symbol">Œª</a> <a id="12484" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12484" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="12486" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a>
      <a id="12494" href="foundation.equivalences.html#26406" class="Function">is-pullback-is-equiv-horizontal-maps</a>
        <a id="12539" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12541" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">_‚àò</a> <a id="12544" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12344" class="Bound">f</a><a id="12545" class="Symbol">)</a>

        <a id="12571" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12573" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.pullback-property-pushouts.html#1402" class="Function">cone-pullback-property-pushout</a> <a id="12604" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12344" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12606" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12346" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="12608" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12394" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="12610" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12484" class="Bound">T</a><a id="12611" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="12621" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12623" href="foundation.universal-property-equivalences.html#1568" class="Function">is-equiv-precomp-is-equiv</a> <a id="12649" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12344" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12651" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12360" class="Bound">is-equiv-f</a> <a id="12662" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12484" class="Bound">T</a><a id="12663" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="12673" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12675" href="foundation.universal-property-equivalences.html#1568" class="Function">is-equiv-precomp-is-equiv</a> <a id="12701" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12353" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="12703" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12371" class="Bound">is-equiv-j</a> <a id="12714" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#12484" class="Bound">T</a><a id="12715" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### If the horizontal map of a span is an equivalence, then the horizontal map of a cocone on it is an equivalence if and only if the cocone is a pushout

### The pushout pasting lemmas

#### The horizontal pushout pasting lemma

If in the following diagram the left square is a pushout, then the outer
rectangle is a pushout if and only if the right square is a pushout.

```text
      g       k
   A ----> B ----> C
   |       |       |
  f|       |       |
   v       v       v
   X ----> Y ----> Z
```

              <a id="20118" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20120" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#18143" class="Bound">up-r</a><a id="20124" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="20140" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20142" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#18286" class="Bound">W</a><a id="20143" class="Symbol">))))</a>
</pre>
#### Extending pushouts by equivalences on the left

As a special case of the horizontal pushout pasting lemma we can extend a
pushout square by equivalences on the left.

If we have a pushout square on the right, equivalences S' ‚âÉ S and A' ‚âÉ A, and a
map f' : S' ‚Üí A' making the left square commute, then the outer rectangle is
again a pushout.

```text
       i       g
   S' ---> S ----> B
   |   ‚âÉ   |       |
f' |       | f     |
   v   ‚âÉ   v     ‚åú v
   A' ---> A ----> X
       j
```

  <a id="20973" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#20973" class="Function">universal-property-pushout-left-extended-by-equivalences</a> <a id="21030" class="Symbol">:</a>

    <a id="21829" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#20973" class="Function">universal-property-pushout-left-extended-by-equivalences</a> <a id="21886" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#21816" class="Bound">ie</a> <a id="21889" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#21819" class="Bound">je</a>
</pre>
#### The vertical pushout pasting lemma

If in the following diagram the top square is a pushout, then the outer
rectangle is a pushout if and only if the bottom square is a pushout.

```text
       g
   A -----> X
   |        |
  f|        |
   v      ‚åú v
   B -----> Y
   |        |
  k|        |
   v        v
   C -----> Z
```

                  <a id="26958" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26960" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#1808" class="Function">horizontal-map-cocone</a> <a id="26982" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22380" class="Bound">k</a>
                    <a id="27004" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27006" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#1808" class="Function">horizontal-map-cocone</a> <a id="27028" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22356" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="27030" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22368" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="27032" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22395" class="Bound">c</a><a id="27033" class="Symbol">)</a>
                    <a id="27055" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27057" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22414" class="Bound">d</a><a id="27058" class="Symbol">))</a>
                  <a id="27079" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27081" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#1940" class="Function">coherence-square-cocone</a> <a id="27105" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22356" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="27107" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22368" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="27109" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22395" class="Bound">c</a><a id="27110" class="Symbol">)</a>
                  <a id="27130" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27132" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#1940" class="Function">coherence-square-cocone</a> <a id="27156" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22380" class="Bound">k</a>
                    <a id="27178" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27180" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#1808" class="Function">horizontal-map-cocone</a> <a id="27202" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22356" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="27204" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22368" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="27206" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22395" class="Bound">c</a><a id="27207" class="Symbol">)</a>
                    <a id="27229" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27231" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22414" class="Bound">d</a><a id="27232" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
            <a id="27250" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27252" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#9281" class="Function">pullback-property-pushout-universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="27305" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27306" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22380" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="27308" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="27310" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22356" class="Bound">f</a><a id="27311" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27313" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22368" class="Bound">g</a>
              <a id="27329" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27331" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#7929" class="Function">cocone-comp-vertical</a> <a id="27352" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22356" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="27354" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22368" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="27356" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22380" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="27358" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22395" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="27360" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#22414" class="Bound">d</a><a id="27361" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="27377" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27379" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#25331" class="Bound">up-r</a><a id="27383" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="27399" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27401" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#25467" class="Bound">W</a><a id="27402" class="Symbol">))))</a>
</pre>
#### Extending pushouts by equivalences at the top

If we have a pushout square on the right, equivalences `S' ‚âÉ S` and `B' ‚âÉ B`,
and a map `g' : S' ‚Üí B'` making the top square commute, then the vertical
rectangle is again a pushout. This is a special case of the vertical pushout
pasting lemma.

```text
           g'
       S' ---> B'
       |       |
     i | ‚âÉ   ‚âÉ | j
       |       |
       v   g   v
       S ----> B
       |       |
     f |       |
       v    ‚åú  v
       A ----> X
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="27917" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="27924" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#27924" class="Module">_</a>

    <a id="28823" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#505" class="Record">Œ£</a> <a id="28825" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28826" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#1443" class="Function">cocone</a> <a id="28833" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28834" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28038" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28836" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="28838" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28062" class="Bound">i</a><a id="28839" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28841" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28088" class="Bound">g&#39;</a> <a id="28844" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#27997" class="Bound">X</a><a id="28845" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28847" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28848" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#2873" class="Function">universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="28875" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28780" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="28877" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28878" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28038" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28880" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="28882" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28062" class="Bound">i</a><a id="28883" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28885" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28088" class="Bound">g&#39;</a><a id="28887" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="28891" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#603" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="28895" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28896" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28716" class="Function">universal-property-pushout-top-extension-by-equivalences</a> <a id="28953" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28953" class="Bound">ie</a> <a id="28956" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28956" class="Bound">je</a><a id="28958" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28960" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="28966" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#8987" class="Function">cocone-comp-vertical&#39;</a> <a id="28988" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28062" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="28990" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28088" class="Bound">g&#39;</a> <a id="28993" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28075" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="28995" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28050" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="28997" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28038" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28999" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28106" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="29001" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28189" class="Bound">coh</a>
  <a id="29007" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="29011" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29012" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28716" class="Function">universal-property-pushout-top-extension-by-equivalences</a> <a id="29069" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29069" class="Bound">ie</a> <a id="29072" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29072" class="Bound">je</a><a id="29074" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29076" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="29082" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#28238" class="Function">universal-property-pushout-top-extended-by-equivalences</a> <a id="29138" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29069" class="Bound">ie</a> <a id="29141" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29072" class="Bound">je</a>
</pre>
### Extending pushouts by equivalences of cocones

Given a commutative diagram where `i`, `j` and `k` are equivalences,

```text
          g'
      S' ---> B'
     / \       \
 f' /   \ k     \ j
   /     v   g   v
  A'     S ----> B
    \    |       |
   i \   | f     |
      \  v     ‚åú v
       > A ----> X
```

the induced square is a pushout:

```text
   S' ---> B'
   |       |
   |       |
   v     ‚åú v
   A' ---> X.
```

This combines both special cases of the pushout pasting lemmas for equivalences.

Notice that the triple `(i,j,k)` is really an equivalence of spans. Thus, this
result can be phrased as: the pushout is invariant under equivalence of spans.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="29827" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="29834" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29834" class="Module">_</a>

      <a id="30607" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30609" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30006" class="Bound">g&#39;</a><a id="30611" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="30671" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30673" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#20973" class="Function">universal-property-pushout-left-extended-by-equivalences</a> <a id="30730" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29967" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="30732" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29979" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="30734" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30050" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="30736" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30024" class="Bound">i</a>
        <a id="30746" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30748" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29991" class="Bound">f&#39;</a><a id="30750" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="30760" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30762" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30066" class="Bound">c</a><a id="30763" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="30773" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30775" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30088" class="Bound">up-c</a><a id="30779" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="30789" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30791" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30149" class="Bound">coh-l</a><a id="30796" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="30806" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30808" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30485" class="Bound">ke</a><a id="30810" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="30820" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30822" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30479" class="Bound">ie</a><a id="30824" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="30833" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30835" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30193" class="Bound">coh-r</a><a id="30840" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="30848" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30850" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#3868" class="Function">is-equiv-id</a><a id="30861" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="30869" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30871" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30482" class="Bound">je</a><a id="30873" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="30878" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30878" class="Function">universal-property-pushout-extended-by-equivalences</a> <a id="30930" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="30936" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1647" class="Function">is-equiv</a> <a id="30945" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30024" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="30947" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="30949" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1647" class="Function">is-equiv</a> <a id="30958" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30037" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="30960" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="30962" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1647" class="Function">is-equiv</a> <a id="30971" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30050" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="30973" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a>
    <a id="30979" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="30980" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30980" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="30982" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30984" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="30989" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="30991" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a>
    <a id="30997" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#2873" class="Function">universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="31024" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30980" class="Bound">l</a>
      <a id="31032" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31034" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29991" class="Bound">f&#39;</a><a id="31036" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="31044" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31046" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30006" class="Bound">g&#39;</a><a id="31048" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="31056" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31058" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cocones-under-spans.html#9906" class="Function">comp-cocone-hom-span</a> <a id="31079" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29967" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="31081" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29979" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="31083" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#29991" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="31086" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30006" class="Bound">g&#39;</a> <a id="31089" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30024" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="31091" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30037" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="31093" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30050" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="31095" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30066" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="31097" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30149" class="Bound">coh-l</a> <a id="31103" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30193" class="Bound">coh-r</a><a id="31108" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="31112" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30878" class="Function">universal-property-pushout-extended-by-equivalences</a> <a id="31164" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#31164" class="Bound">ie</a> <a id="31167" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#31167" class="Bound">je</a> <a id="31170" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#31170" class="Bound">ke</a> <a id="31173" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="31179" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="31183" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31184" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#30244" class="Function">universal-property-pushout-extension-by-equivalences</a> <a id="31237" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#31164" class="Bound">ie</a> <a id="31240" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#31167" class="Bound">je</a> <a id="31243" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#31170" class="Bound">ke</a><a id="31245" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### In a commuting cube where the vertical maps are equivalences, the bottom square is a pushout if and only if the top square is a pushout

<pre class="Agda"><a id="31401" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="31408" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.universal-property-pushouts.html#31408" class="Module">_</a>
